# Graph Report - .  (2026-07-04)

## Corpus Check
- Large corpus: 9599 files · ~8,546,417 words. Semantic extraction will be expensive (many Claude tokens). Consider running on a subfolder.

- 44464 nodes · 96846 edges · 1898 communities (1726 shown, 172 thin omitted)
- Extraction: 89% EXTRACTED · 11% INFERRED · 0% AMBIGUOUS · INFERRED: 10998 edges (avg confidence: 0.62)
- Token cost: 0 input · 0 output
